<script>
    var setDisplayHelp = function() {
        var showStaticHelp = "Search box will always been displayed.";
        var showDynamicHelp = "Users will be able to toggle the search box visibility.";
        var selectedDisplayType = $('#display-type-select-_9Iz7WPMNFvBe').val();
        if(selectedDisplayType == 'static') {
            $('#display-type-select-help-_9Iz7WPMNFvBe').html(showStaticHelp);
        } else {
            $('#display-type-select-help-_9Iz7WPMNFvBe').html(showDynamicHelp);
        }
    }
    
    var validateSubmitSearchForm = function(e) { 
        // Validate if text was inputted before submitting
        var searchText = $("#cs-search-field-_9Iz7WPMNFvBe").val().trim();
        if(searchText != "" && searchText != undefined) {
            // remove the has error
            $('#cs-search-view-form-_9Iz7WPMNFvBe .input-group').removeClass('has-error');
            // sanitize the field before submitting 
            if($.sanitize) $("#cs-search-field-_9Iz7WPMNFvBe").val($.sanitize(searchText));
            $('#cs-search-view-form-_9Iz7WPMNFvBe').submit();
        } else {
            e.preventDefault();
            // add has-error class to the form
            $('#cs-search-view-form-_9Iz7WPMNFvBe .input-group').addClass('has-error');
            $("#cs-search-field-_9Iz7WPMNFvBe").focus();
        }
    }

   $(document).ready(function() {
       var displayMode = 'static';
       displayMode = displayMode == '' ? 'static' : displayMode;
       $('#display-type-select-_9Iz7WPMNFvBe option[value="'+displayMode+'"]').attr("selected", "selected");

        setDisplayHelp();

        $('#display-type-select-_9Iz7WPMNFvBe').change(function() {
             setDisplayHelp();
        });

       $('.cs-search-view-dynamic').click(function() {
            if($('.down-search-arrow').is(':visible')) {
                $('.down-search-arrow').hide();
                $('.up-search-arrow').show();
                $('#cs-search-view-form-_9Iz7WPMNFvBe').slideDown(300);
            } else {
                $('.down-search-arrow').show();
                $('.up-search-arrow').hide();
                $('#cs-search-view-form-_9Iz7WPMNFvBe').slideUp(300);
            }
       });
       
       // checks whether the pressed key is "Enter", and performs search if so
        $("#cs-search-field-_9Iz7WPMNFvBe").keypress(function(e) {
            if(e.which == 13) { 
                validateSubmitSearchForm(e);
            }
        });

      $('#cs-search-field-_9Iz7WPMNFvBe + span').click(function(e) { 
            validateSubmitSearchForm(e);
      });
       
       
   });
</script>

</tbody>
</table>
</div>
<div class="entry-links">

<div class="aui-w65 portlet-column" id="column-4">
<div class="portlet-dropzone portlet-column-content" id="layout-column_column-4">
<div class="portlet-boundary portlet-boundary_56_ portlet-static portlet-static-end portlet-borderless portlet-journal-content " id="p_p_id_56_INSTANCE_Z06so4VRxxmR_">
<span id="p_56_INSTANCE_Z06so4VRxxmR"></span>
<div class="portlet-body">
<div class="portlet-borderless-container" style="">
<div class="portlet-body">
<div class="journal-content-article">
<span style="line-height: 1.4;">SWEBOK V3.0 is the most recent completely revised and updated version of the internationally respected Guide to the <em>Software Engineering Body of Knowledge</em>. Newly imagined as a living, changing document, and thoroughly rewritten, SWEBOK V3.0 has been developed and created by leading authorities, reviewed by professionals, and made available for public review and comment, continuing its 20-year reputation as the most authoritative, fundamental, and trusted definition of the software engineering profession.</span>
<div>
	Â </div>
<div>
	SWEBOK V3.0 is comprised of 15 Knowledge Areas, plus a new Appendix on Standards.</div>
<div>
	Â </div>
<div>
	SWEBOK V3.0 is now specifically designed to be constantly reviewed and updated as technology and the engineering profession changes over time, remaining consistently relevant. Be sure to register to receive notifications when the SWEBOK Guide is revised.</div>
<div>
	Â </div>
<div>
	The citation information for SWEBOK V3.0 is as follows:</div>
<div>
	Â </div>
<div>
	P. Bourque and R.E. Fairley, eds.,<em> Guide to the Software Engineering Body of Knowledge, Version 3.0</em>, IEEE Computer Society, 2014; <a href="http://www.swebok.org" target="_blank">www.swebok.org</a>.</div>
</div>
<div class="entry-links">
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="portlet-boundary portlet-boundary_56_ portlet-static portlet-static-end portlet-borderless portlet-journal-content " id="p_p_id_56_INSTANCE_piOh8YZ8Zq6G_">
<span id="p_56_INSTANCE_piOh8YZ8Zq6G"></span>
<div class="portlet-body">
<div class="portlet-borderless-container" style="">
<div class="portlet-body">
<div class="journal-content-article">
<h2>
	Why a SWEBOK Version 3?</h2>
<p>
<span style="line-height: 1.4;">Early on, the committee in charge of the 2004 SWEBOK Guide knew it had to plan for revisions, and in fact outlined a process for doing so in Appendix B of the 2004 Guide. There are many reasons for doing so, including the following:</span></p>
<ul>
<li>
<span style="line-height: 1.4;"><strong>Practices change.</strong> New tools, methods, and types of software make good practice in software engineering an ever-changing target. Topics that were once experimental may have now reached the state of generally accepted knowledge. And even though the Guide focuses on the most widely accepted and long-lasting of practices, it's possible for the environment that software operates in to change significantly because of business and job changes. For example, it has become clear in just the past few years that good software practice must pay increasing attention to security. Economics can also affect what methods become best practices in software engineering.</span></li>
<li>
<strong>Other viewpoints emerge. </strong>Other Computer Society productsâ€”notably the Certified Software Development Professional (CSDP) exam and the Software Engineering 2004 curriculum guideâ€”offer slightly differing views of the body of knowledge. So it makes sense to take the opportunity to examine them and better align the SWEBOK Version 3 with them where it makes sense. For example, it seems reasonable that there should be a core set of references for these products, so part of the work on the SWEBOK Version 3 will establish that core set. The comparison among these efforts has also suggested the need for new knowledge areas and the revision of others.</li>
<li>
<strong>The body of knowledge grows.</strong> Since 2004, many of the books cited in the first SWEBOK Guide have been revised and new articles have been added to the body of knowledge. The SWEBOK Version 3 should account for these changes.</li>
</ul>
<p>
	These factors drive the need for a new version of the SWEBOK Guide.</p>
</div>
<div class="entry-links">
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>

                      beforeSend: function() {
